fixMagicPointer()

0DD5: CURRENT_PLATFORM = get_platform
hPlayer = Player.GetActor(hChar)
hGroup = Player.GetGroup(hChar)

ResetVars()
Widget_ResetPositions()
if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
then jump @MainLoop_PC
else jump @MainLoop_Android
end

:MainLoop_PC
    if Key.IsPressed(VK.O)
    then Menu_Open()
    end
    Wait0()
jump @MainLoop_PC

:MainLoop_Android
    if Widget.IsPressed(91) 
    then Menu_Open()
    end
    Wait0()
jump @MainLoop_Android

:testInt 
    if Key.IsPressed(0@)
    then 2@ += 1
    end
    if Key.IsPressed(1@)
    then 2@ -= 1
    end
ret 1 2@

:testFloat 
    if Key.IsPressed(0@)
    then 2@ += 1.0
    end
    if Key.IsPressed(1@)
    then 2@ -= 1.0
    end
ret 1 2@

:testFloatTin 
    if Key.IsPressed(0@)
    then 2@ += 0.1
    end
    if Key.IsPressed(1@)
    then 2@ -= 0.1
    end
ret 1 2@

:MutexVar_Set 
    FixUpdate()
    if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    then set_cleo_shared_var 0@ = 1@
    else set_mutex_var 0@ = 1@
    end
ret 0

:MutexVar_Get 
    FixUpdate()
    if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    then get_cleo_shared_var 1@ = 0@
    else get_mutex_var 1@ = 0@
    end
ret 1 1@

:get_bit_status
    if 08B9:   test 0@ bit 1@
    then ret 1 true
    else ret 1 false
    end 
return

:ResetVars
    Text.ClearHelp()
    IFP_FILE = 0
    IFP_ANIM = 0
    THROTTLE_INTERVAL = 200
    WAIT_DEFAULT = 200
    WAIT_INFO = 700
    WAIT_ERROR = 3000
    WAIT_DEBUG = 100
    
    DYOS_VERSION = DYOS_CODE_VERSION

    PLAYER_FLAGS = 0
	bit_set_true  PLAYER_FLAGS PLAYER_PROP_COLISION
	bit_set_false PLAYER_FLAGS PLAYER_PROP_IMMUNITION_BULLETS
	bit_set_false PLAYER_FLAGS PLAYER_PROP_IMMUNITION_FIRE
	bit_set_false PLAYER_FLAGS PLAYER_PROP_IMMUNITION_EXPLOSION

:GET_TIMER
    FixUpdate()
    if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    then 0@ = TIMERA
    else 0@ = TIMERX
    end
ret 1 0@

:ON_MISSION
    if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    then
        if $409 == true
        then return
        end
    else
        if $408 == true
        then return
        end
    end
return

LAST_THROTTLE_TIME = 0
:throttle
	
    
    20@ = Game.GetCurrentTimeMs()
	int 21@ = 20@ - LAST_THROTTLE_TIME
	if
		21@ >= THROTTLE_INTERVAL
	then
		
		LAST_THROTTLE_TIME = 20@
		return
	else
		return
	end
return

	printf "%i~n~~g~%s~s~/%s" 100 CURRENT_ANIM_ID IFP_FILE IFP_ANIM

	if Menu_Select()
	then break
	end
	if Menu_Return()
	then
		Actor.SetClearTasks(hPlayer)
		PLAYER_ANIM_LIB = PLAYER_ANIM_LIB_NONE
		break
	end
end

                    if SMX_BUFFER_MAIN <> 0
                    then 0AC9: free_allocated_memory SMX_BUFFER_MAIN
                    end

                    0A9C: FILE_SIZE = file FILE_HANDLE size

                    0AC8: SMX_BUFFER_MAIN = allocate_memory_size FILE_SIZE

                    while FILE_OFFSET < FILE_SIZE
                        0AD5: file_seek FILE_HANDLE offset FILE_OFFSET origin 0
                        0A9D: read_file FILE_HANDLE size 1 to 0@

                        2402: write_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_MAIN offset FILE_OFFSET size 1 value 0@
                        FILE_OFFSET += 1
                    end
                    FILE_OFFSET = 0

                    Menu_Display_Hide()

                    
                    
                    
                    if FILE_SIZE == 0
                    then
                        printf "file not writed" WAIT_ERROR
                        
                        goto @read_found_error
                    else
                        if or
                            FILE_OFFSET == FILE_SIZE
                            FILE_SIZE == 4
                        then
                            printf "file in white" WAIT_ERROR
                            
                            goto @read_found_error
                        end

                        Player_GetLastPosition()

                        if not Actor.IsDriving(hPlayer)
                        then Actor.SetCollisionDetection(hPlayer) = true
                        end
                        Player.SetCanMove(hChar) = true

                        while true
                            3@ = Game.GetCurrentTimeMs()
                            3@ -= 2@
                            if 3@ > 0@
                            then break
                            end
                            Wait0()
                            3@ /= 1000
                            1@ = 3 - 3@

                        end

                        read_buffer_int()
                        FILE_VERSION = SMX_A

                        printf "dyos_version: %i~n~file_version: %i" WAIT_INFO DYOS_VERSION FILE_VERSION
                        call @waitPlis 1 WAIT_INFO

                        SMX_IF_ACTIVE = 0
                        SMX_ENTER_CONDITION = false
                        SMX_COMMAND_IS_CONDITIONAL = 0
                        SMX_COND_START_OFFSET  = 0

                        SMX_NUM_ACTORS = 0
                        SMX_INDEX_ACTORS = 0

                        SMX_ACTOR_TO_KILL = 0

                        hPlayer = Player.GetActor(0)
                        hGroup = Player.GetGroup(0)

                        while SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET < FILE_SIZE
                            wait0()

                            
                            read_buffer_cmd()

                            SMX_read_command()
                        end

                        
                        
                        call @clear_buffer 1 BUFFER_ACTORS

                        Text.ClearHelp()
                        Display.SetRadar(false)
                        if not Actor.IsDriving(hPlayer)
                        then Actor.SetCollisionDetection(hPlayer) = false
                        end
                        Player.SetCanMove(hChar) = false
                        Player_RemindPosition()
                        Actor.GetPosition(hPlayer, SMX_Af, SMX_Bf, SMX_Cf)
                        call @ClearArea_Radius 4 SMX_Af SMX_Bf SMX_Cf 100.0
                        Actor.SetHealth(hPlayer) = 100
                    end

                    printf "finish, closed file" WAIT_INFO
                    call @waitPlis 1 WAIT_INFO
                    
                    Menu_Display_Show()
                    jump @Menu_Mission
                else
                    printf "file not exist" WAIT_ERROR
                    call @waitPlis 2 WAIT_ERROR false
                end

                Menu.SetActiveItem(hPanel, 2)
                jump @Menu_Mission

            case 3 

                Menu.SetColumn(hPanel, 0, 'M0000A1','M0000A0','M00009Z',none,none,none,none,none,none,none,none,none,none)
                Menu_Take_Return()
                Menu_Take_Selection()
                repeat
                    if Menu_Enter()
                    then
                        if _SELECTED == 0
                        then goto @Menu_Mission
                        end

                        if _SELECTED == 1
                        then
                            reset_file()
                            Menu.SetItemWithNumber(hPanel, 1, 1, 'M00000]', 4) 
                            break
                        end
                    end
                until Menu_Return()

                Menu.SetActiveItem(hPanel, 4)
                jump @Menu_Mission
            default
                Text.PrintHelp('M0000WQ') 
                Menu.SetActiveItem(hPanel, _SELECTED)
                jump @Menu_Mission
        end
    end
until Menu_Return()  
setMenuClear()
Menu.SetActiveItem(hPanel, MENU_MISSION)
jump @Menu_iMain

:File_Chech_Exist
    if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    then DIR_DYOS = "CLEO/DYOS/#0"
    else DIR_DYOS = "/DYOS/#0"
    end
    if 0AAB:  does_file_exist DIR_DYOS
    then
        FILE_EXIST = true
        
        0A9A: FILE_HANDLE = DIR_DYOS "rb"
        0A9C: FILE_SIZE = file FILE_HANDLE size
        0A9B: file_close FILE_HANDLE
    else
        if 0A9A: FILE_HANDLE = DIR_DYOS "rb"
        then
            Fs.Close(FILE_HANDLE)
            FILE_EXIST = true
        else
            Text.PrintHelp('M00001?') 

            if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
            then
                if 8AE4: directory_exist "CLEO/DYOS/"
                then
                    if 0AE5: create_directory "CLEO/DYOS/" 
                    then call @waitPlis 1 150
                    end
                end
            else
                if 8AE4: directory_exist "DYOS/"
                then
                    if 0AE5: create_directory "DYOS/" 
                    then call @waitPlis 1 150
                    end
                end
            end

            if 0A9A: FILE_HANDLE = DIR_DYOS "w+b"
            then
                call @waitPlis 1 150
                0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 from 0 
                call @waitPlis 1 150
                Fs.Close(FILE_HANDLE)
                call @waitPlis 1 150

                FILE_EXIST = true

                if 0AAB:  does_file_exist DIR_DYOS
                then
                    reset_file()
                    Text.ClearHelp()
                    Text.PrintHelp('M00001_') 
                    goto @File_Chech_Exist
                end
            end

            FILE_EXIST = false
            Text.PrintHelp('M00000+') 
        end
    end
return

:read_buffer_cmd
    2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_MAIN offset SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET size 4 store_to FILE_COMMAND
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET += 4
return

:read_buffer_int
    2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_MAIN offset SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_A
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET += 4
return

:read_buffer_float
    2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_MAIN offset SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_Af
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET += 4
return

:read_buffer_3_int
    2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_MAIN offset SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_A
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET += 4
    2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_MAIN offset SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_B
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET += 4
    2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_MAIN offset SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_C
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET += 4
return

:read_buffer_3_float
    2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_MAIN offset SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_Af
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET += 4
    2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_MAIN offset SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_Bf
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET += 4
    2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_MAIN offset SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_Cf
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET += 4
return

:read_found_error
    Display.SetRadar(false)
    if not Actor.IsDriving(hPlayer)
    then Actor.SetCollisionDetection(hPlayer) = false
    end
    Player.SetCanMove(hChar) = false
    Menu_Display_Show()
    Player_RemindPosition()
    Menu.SetActiveItem(hPanel, 2)
goto @Menu_Mission

:reset_file
    if 0A9A: FILE_HANDLE = DIR_DYOS "wb"
    then
        FILE_OFFSET = 0
        
        
        
        
        
        0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 from DYOS_CODE_VERSION
        Fs.Close(FILE_HANDLE)
    end
return

:clear_buffer
    
    
    

    int 0@
    int 1@

    int 5@ = 0
    int 6@ = 0
    
    fixMagicPointer()
    if 0@ == BUFFER_ACTORS
    then
        while SMX_NUM_ACTORS > 0
            call @SMX_Array_Actor_Get 2 SMX_NUM_ACTORS B_ACTOR_HANDLE result SMX_ACTOR

            if Actor.Defined(SMX_ACTOR)
            then Actor.Remove(SMX_ACTOR)
            end

            call @SMX_Array_Actor_Set 3 SMX_NUM_ACTORS B_ACTOR_HANDLE value 0

            SMX_NUM_ACTORS -= 1
        end
        goto @exit_clear_buffer
    end

    :exit_clear_buffer
ret 0

:SMX_read_command

if FILE_COMMAND >= 0x8000
then SMX_IF_ACTIVE = 1
end

switch FILE_COMMAND

case VM_WAIT

    read_buffer_int()
    call @waitPlis 2 SMX_A false

case VM_GOTO

    read_buffer_int()
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET = SMX_A

case VM_IF

    read_buffer_int()
    SMX_IF_TYPE = SMX_A        
    read_buffer_int()
    SMX_IF_FALSE_JUMP = SMX_A  

    
    if SMX_IF_ACTIVE == 1
    then
        if SMX_IF_TYPE == 0 
        then
            if SMX_CONT_CONDITION <> SMX_IF_TRUE
            then
                SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET = SMX_IF_FALSE_JUMP
            end
        else 
            if SMX_CONT_CONDITION == 0
            then
                SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET = SMX_IF_FALSE_JUMP
            end
        end
    end

    SMX_IF_ACTIVE = 0
    SMX_IF_TRUE = 0
    SMX_CONT_CONDITION = 0

    if SMX_ACTOR_TO_KILL > 0
    then printf "sleep to %i actors" 84 SMX_ACTOR_TO_KILL
    end

    SMX_ACTOR_TO_KILL = 0

case VM_END_THREAD

    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET = FILE_SIZE

case VM_NOP

    nop

case VM_PLAYER_SET_POSITION

    read_buffer_3_float()
    Actor.SetPosition(hPlayer,SMX_Af,SMX_Bf,SMX_Cf)

case VM_PLAYER_SET_WANTED

    read_buffer_int()
    Player.SetWantedLevel(hChar) = SMX_A

case VM_PLAYER_SET_WEAPON

    read_buffer_int()
    
    read_buffer_3_int()
    call @GiveWeaponAndAmmo 4 actor hPlayer model_id SMX_A weapon_id SMX_B ammo SMX_C

case VM_PLAYER_SET_ANIM

    read_buffer_3_int()

    CURRENT_ANIM_ID = SMX_B
    if SMX_A == PLAYER_ANIM_LIB_DYOM
    then AnimDyom()
    end
    if SMX_A == PLAYER_ANIM_LIB_DYOS
    then AnimDyos()
    end
    
    if ANIM_NOT_IS_OF_PED == false
    then
        if lbit_run SMX_C PLAYER_PROP_COLISION
        then Task.PlayAnimSecondary(hPlayer, IFP_ANIM, "PED", 30.0, true, false, false, false, -1)
        else Task.PlayAnim(hPlayer, IFP_ANIM, "PED", 30.0, true, false, false, false, -1)
        end
    else
        Animation.Load(IFP_FILE)
        repeat
            Wait0()
        until Animation.Available(IFP_FILE)
        if lbit_run SMX_C PLAYER_PROP_COLISION
        then Task.PlayAnimSecondary(hPlayer, IFP_ANIM, IFP_FILE, 4.0, true, false, false, false, -1)
        else Task.PlayAnim(hPlayer, IFP_ANIM, IFP_FILE, 4.0, true, false, false, false, -1)
        end
        Animation.Remove(IFP_FILE)
    end

case VM_PLAYER_SET_FIGHT

    read_buffer_int()
    Actor.SetFightStyle(hPlayer, SMX_A, 6)
    
case VM_PLAYER_SET_HEALTH

    read_buffer_int()
    Actor.SetHealth(hPlayer) = SMX_A

case VM_ACTOR_CREATE
    SMX_NUM_ACTORS += 1

    read_buffer_int() 
    call @SMX_Array_Actor_Set 3 SMX_NUM_ACTORS B_ACTOR_ID value SMX_A

    read_buffer_int() 
    SMX_G = SMX_A
    read_buffer_int() 
    ACTOR_MODEL_REQ = SMX_A

    read_buffer_3_float() 
    SMX_Hf = SMX_Af
    SMX_If = SMX_Bf
    SMX_Jf = SMX_Cf
    read_buffer_float()  
    SMX_Kf = SMX_Af

    0@ = undefined
    CargarActorModelo()

    0980: extinguish_all_fires_at SMX_Hf SMX_If SMX_Jf 1.0

    if and
        ACTOR_MODEL_REQ >= 0
        ACTOR_MODEL_REQ < 1000
    then
        Actor.Create(SMX_ACTOR, SMX_G, ACTOR_MODEL_REQ, SMX_Hf, SMX_If, SMX_Jf)
        Model.Release(ACTOR_MODEL_REQ)
    else
        Actor.Create(SMX_ACTOR, PedType.Special, #SPECIAL01, SMX_Hf, SMX_If, SMX_Jf)
        SpecialActor.Release(1)
    end
    call @SMX_Array_Actor_Set 3 SMX_NUM_ACTORS B_ACTOR_HANDLE value SMX_ACTOR

    Actor.Angle(SMX_ACTOR) = SMX_Kf

    if DYOS_VERSION > 300010
    then
        read_buffer_int() 
        TEMP_FLAGS = SMX_A
        call @SMX_Array_Actor_Set 3 SMX_NUM_ACTORS B_ACTOR_FLAGS TEMP_FLAGS

        if lbit_is_true TEMP_FLAGS ACTOR_PROP_CROUCH
        then Task.PlayAnim(SMX_ACTOR,"WEAPON_crouch", "PED", 1000.0, true, false, false, false, -1)
        end

        read_buffer_int() 
        call @Weapon_GetModelID 1 SMX_A result SMX_B
        if SMX_B <> 0 
        then
            Model.Load(SMX_B)
            Model.Requested()

            repeat
                Wait0()
            until Model.Available(SMX_B)

            Actor.setGiveWeaponAndAmmo(SMX_ACTOR, SMX_A, 999)
            
            Model.Release(SMX_B)
        end
    end 

case VM_TASK_KILL_PLAYER

    read_buffer_int() 
    call @SMX_Get_Index_Actor 1 SMX_A result SMX_INDEX_ACTORS

    if SMX_INDEX_ACTORS <> 0
    then
        call @SMX_Array_Actor_Get 2 SMX_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_HANDLE value SMX_ACTOR
        
        if Actor.Defined(SMX_ACTOR)
        then
            Task.KillActorOnFoot(SMX_ACTOR, hPlayer)

            read_buffer_int()
            call @SMX_Array_Actor_Set 3 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS SMX_INDEX_ACTORS SMX_A
            Actor.SetWeaponAccuracy(SMX_ACTOR) = SMX_A

            read_buffer_float()
            call @SMX_Array_Actor_Set 3 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS SMX_INDEX_ACTORS SMX_Af
            Actor.SetMeleeAccuracy(SMX_ACTOR) = SMX_Af

            read_buffer_int()
            call @SMX_Array_Actor_Set 3 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS SMX_INDEX_ACTORS SMX_A
            Actor.SetAttackRate(SMX_ACTOR) = SMX_A

            printf "tarea aplicada" 2000
            call @waitPlis 1 2000
        end
    end

case VM_PLAYER_IS_POSITION
    read_buffer_3_float()
    
    
    

    SMX_CONT_CONDITION += 1

    SMX_TEMP_OFFSET = SMX_CONT_CONDITION * 4

    if Actor.Defined(hPlayer)
    then

        2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_TARGET_BLIPS offset SMX_TEMP_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_TARGET_BLIP
        2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_TARGET_SPHERES offset SMX_TEMP_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_TARGET_SPHERE

        if SMX_TARGET_BLIP == 0
        then
            SMX_TARGET_BLIP = Blip.Create(SMX_Af, SMX_Bf, SMX_Cf, 1, 1)
            0165: set_marker SMX_TARGET_BLIP color_to 0
            0168: show_on_radar SMX_TARGET_BLIP size 3
            018B: show_on_radar SMX_TARGET_BLIP in 3

            SMX_TARGET_SPHERE = Sphere.Create(SMX_Af, SMX_Bf, SMX_Cf, 2.0)
            2402: write_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_TARGET_BLIPS offset SMX_TEMP_OFFSET size 4 value SMX_TARGET_BLIP
            2402: write_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_TARGET_SPHERES offset SMX_TEMP_OFFSET size 4 value SMX_TARGET_SPHERE
        end

        if Actor.IsLocated3D(hPlayer, 0, SMX_Af, SMX_Bf, SMX_Cf, 1.0, 1.0, 3.0)
        then
            SMX_IF_TRUE += 1

            Blip.Remove(SMX_TARGET_BLIP)
            Sphere.Remove(SMX_TARGET_SPHERE)
            2402: write_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_TARGET_BLIPS offset SMX_TEMP_OFFSET size 4 value 0
            2402: write_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_TARGET_SPHERES offset SMX_TEMP_OFFSET size 4 value 0
        end
    
        printf "goto the red circle~n~ to %.2f %.2f %.2f" 84 SMX_Af SMX_Bf SMX_Cf
    else
        SMX_IF_TRUE += 1
    end

case VM_PLAYER_IS_KILL_TO_ACTOR

    read_buffer_int() 
    call @SMX_Get_Index_Actor 1 id SMX_A index SMX_INDEX_ACTORS

    if SMX_INDEX_ACTORS <> 0
    then
        call @SMX_Array_Actor_Get 2 SMX_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_HANDLE value SMX_ACTOR

        SMX_CONT_CONDITION += 1
        SMX_TEMP_OFFSET = SMX_CONT_CONDITION * 4
        
        if Actor.Defined(SMX_ACTOR)
        then
            SMX_ACTOR_TO_KILL += 1

            2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_TARGET_BLIPS offset SMX_TEMP_OFFSET size 4 store_to SMX_TARGET_BLIP
            
            if SMX_TARGET_BLIP == 0
            then
                0187: SMX_TARGET_BLIP = create_marker_above_actor SMX_ACTOR
                0165: set_marker SMX_TARGET_BLIP color_to 0
                0168: show_on_radar SMX_TARGET_BLIP size 3
                018B: show_on_radar SMX_TARGET_BLIP in 3

                2402: write_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_TARGET_BLIPS offset SMX_TEMP_OFFSET size 4 value SMX_TARGET_BLIP
            end

            if Actor.IsDead(SMX_ACTOR)
            then
                SMX_IF_TRUE += 1
                SMX_ACTOR_TO_KILL -= 1

                Blip.Remove(SMX_TARGET_BLIP)
                2402: write_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_TARGET_BLIPS offset SMX_TEMP_OFFSET size 4 value 0
            end
        else
            SMX_IF_TRUE += 1
        end
    end

default
    nop
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET -= 4
    printf "ERROR:~n~UNKNOW COMMAND: %x~n~OFFSET: %i" WAIT_ERROR FILE_COMMAND SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET
    call @waitPlis 1 WAIT_ERROR
    SMX_CURRENT_OFFSET = FILE_SIZE
end

return

:SMX_write_command
if FILE_COMMAND >= 0x8000
then
    if SMX_ENTER_CONDITION == false
    then
        SMX_ENTER_CONDITION = true

        SMX_START_CONDITION = FILE_SIZE
    end
else
    SMX_ENTER_CONDITION = false
end

if FILE_COMMAND >= 0x8000
then
    
    if SMX_IN_CONDITION_BLOCK == false
    then
        SMX_IN_CONDITION_BLOCK = true
        SMX_IF_EMITTED = false
        SMX_COND_START_OFFSET = FILE_SIZE
    end
else
    
    if SMX_IN_CONDITION_BLOCK == true
    then
        if SMX_IF_EMITTED == false
        then
            
            0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to VM_IF
            0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to 0  
            0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_COND_START_OFFSET

            SMX_IF_EMITTED = true
        end

        SMX_IN_CONDITION_BLOCK = false
    end
end

0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to FILE_COMMAND

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_WAIT
then
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A 
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_GOTO
then
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A 
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_NOP
then nop
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_END_THREAD
then nop
end

    

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_SET_WANTED
then
    0@ = Player.GetWantedLevel(hChar)
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_SET_WEAPON
then
    SMX_A = Actor.GetCurrentWeapon(hPlayer)
    SMX_B = Actor.GetWeaponAmmo(hPlayer, SMX_A)
    call @Weapon_GetModelID 1 SMX_A ret SMX_H

    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to -1 

    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_H 
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A 
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_B 
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_ADD_AMMON
then nop
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_SET_ANIM
then
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to PLAYER_ANIM_LIB
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to PLAYER_ANIM_ID
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to PLAYER_FLAGS
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_SET_FIGHT
then
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to PLAYER_FIGHT
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_SET_HEALTH
then
    SMX_A = Actor.GetHealth(hPlayer)
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_SET_ARMOUR
then nop
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_SET_COORDS
then nop
end

    

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_ACTOR_CREATE
then
    call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_ID value SMX_A
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A

    SMX_A = Actor.GetPedtype(SPS_ACTOR)
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A

    call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_MODEL result SMX_A
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A
    
    Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(SMX_Af,SMX_Bf,SMX_Cf,SPS_ACTOR,0.0,0.0,-1.0)
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_Af
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_Bf
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_Cf

    SMX_Af = Actor.GetAngle(SPS_ACTOR)
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_Af

    if DYOS_VERSION > 300010
    then
        call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_FLAGS SMX_A
        0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A

        SMX_A = Actor.GetCurrentWeapon(SPS_ACTOR)
        0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A
    end
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_TASK_KILL_PLAYER
then
    call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_ID value SMX_A
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A

    
    call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_ACU_DIST SMX_A
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A
    
    
    call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_ACU_DIST SMX_Af
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_Af
    
    
    call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_ACU_DIST SMX_A
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A
    
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_IF
then
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to 0 
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_START_CONDITION 
end

if or
    FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_IS_POSITION
    FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_SET_POSITION
then
    Actor.GetPosition(hPlayer,SMX_Af,SMX_Bf,SMX_Cf)
    SMX_Cf -= 1.0
    
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_Af 
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_Bf 
    0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_Cf 
end

if FILE_COMMAND == VM_PLAYER_IS_KILL_TO_ACTOR
then 0A9E: write_file FILE_HANDLE size 4 to SMX_A 
end

FILE_COMMAND = -1

Aplicated()
return

                    else
                        Text.PrintHelp('M00000+')
                    end

                default
                    Text.PrintHelp('M0000WQ') 
            end

            Menu_Take_Selection()
        end
    until Menu_Return()

    :Menu_Close
    
    Menu_Display_Hide()
    Display.SetRadar(true)

    Menu_Take_Return()

    if not Actor.IsDriving(hPlayer)
    then Actor.SetCollisionDetection(hPlayer) = true
    end
    if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    then
        if Actor.IsDriving(hPlayer)
        then Menu_Take_Return()
        end
    end
    Player.SetCanMove(hChar) = true

    Text.UseCommands(false)

    Text.ClearHelp()
return

:Menu_Display_Hide
	Menu.Remove(hPanel)
	Display.SetRadar(true)

	call @Buffer_Var_Set 2 B_VAR_MENU_DISPLAY = MENU_DISPLAY_NONE
return

:Menu_Display_Show
	hPanel = Menu.Create(none, 29.0, 154.0, 160.0, 2, true, true, Align.Left)
	Menu.SetColumnWidth(hPanel, 1, 40)
	Menu.SetColumnAlignment(hPanel,1,Align.Center)

	Display.SetRadar(false)
	if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
	then 
		Menu.SetColumnWidth(hPanel,0,160)
		Text.SetHelpMessageBoxSize(218)
	end

	call @Buffer_Var_Set 2 B_VAR_MENU_DISPLAY = MENU_DISPLAY_BLOCK
return

:Menu_Print_Pagination

    call @Buffer_Var_Get 1 B_VAR_MENU_DISPLAY = 0@
    if 0@ == MENU_DISPLAY_BLOCK
    then
    	

    	Text.SetCenter(true)
    	if CURRENT_PAGE > NUMBER_PAGE
    	then CURRENT_PAGE = NUMBER_PAGE
    	end
    	if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    	then Text.DisplayWith2Numbers(210.0,179.0,'M0000BG',CURRENT_PAGE,NUMBER_PAGE)
    	else Text.DisplayWith2Numbers(150.0,179.0,'M0000BG',CURRENT_PAGE,NUMBER_PAGE)
    	end
    	call @ShowData 0
    	
    	
    	if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    	then
    		if not Actor.IsDriving(hPlayer)
    		then
    			Player_GetLastPosition()
    			Actor.Angle(hPlayer) = tempvar_Angle
    		end
    	end
    	
    	if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    	then
            Txd.DrawRect(533.0, 394.0, 203.0, 96.0, 0,0,0,100)
            Text.SetScale(0.3, 1.7)
            Text.SetBackground(false)
            if NUMBER_PAGE == 1
            then Text.DisplayWithNumber(440.0, 350.0, 'M00000?', 0) 
            else Text.DisplayWithNumber(440.0, 350.0, 'M00000%', 0) 
            end
        end
        
        Change_Debug_Mode()
        
        if DYOS_HELP_ID == 1
then HELP_SCM = "M00000'" 
end

if DYOS_HELP_ID == 2
then HELP_SCM = "M00000." 
end

if DYOS_HELP_ID == 3
then HELP_SCM = "M00000," 
end

if DYOS_HELP_ID == 4
then HELP_SCM = "M00000:" 
end

if DYOS_HELP_ID == 5
then HELP_SCM = "M00000;" 
end

if DYOS_HELP_ID == 6
then HELP_SCM = "M00000<" 
end

if DYOS_HELP_ID == 7
then HELP_SCM = "M00001{" 
end

if DYOS_HELP_ID <> 0
then
	Text.SetWrapX(600.0)
	Text.Display(438.0, 320.0, HELP_SCM)
	Txd.DrawRect(532.0, 326.0, 203.0, 26.0, 0,0,0,100)
end

DYOS_HELP_ID = 0

    end
return

:CustomSkin4
	int 0@ 

		call @label_addr 1 label @LoadCustomSkinS1 result 1@
		
    1@ += 5 

    2@ = 1 
    while 2@ <= 6
    	
    	3@ = 1@ + 2@ 
		call @MemoryWrite 3 3@ emCHAR 0x00
	    2@++
	end

	int 3@ 
	if 0@ > 0
	then 3@ = 1
	end
	if 0@ > 9
	then 3@ = 2
	end
	if 0@ > 99
	then 3@ = 3
	end
	if 0@ > 999
	then 3@ = 4
	end

	if 3@ >= 4
    then
    	12@ = 1@ + 4
    	call @Math4_Module 2 0@ 10 0@ 7@
    	7@ += 0x30
    	call @MemoryWrite 3 12@ emCHAR 7@
    else
    	7@ = -1
    end
	if 3@ >= 3
    then
    	12@ = 1@ + 3
    	call @Math4_Module 2 0@ 10 0@ 6@
    	6@ += 0x30
    	call @MemoryWrite 3 12@ emCHAR 6@
    else
    	6@ = -1
    end
	if 3@ >= 2
    then
    	12@ = 1@ + 2
    	call @Math4_Module 2 0@ 10 0@ 5@
    	5@ += 0x30
    	call @MemoryWrite 3 12@ emCHAR 5@
    else
    	5@ = -1
    end
	if 3@ >= 1
    then
    	12@ = 1@ + 1
    	call @Math4_Module 2 0@ 10 0@ 4@
    	4@ += 0x30
    	call @MemoryWrite 3 12@ emCHAR 4@
    else
    	4@ = -1
    end

	:LoadCustomSkinS1
	SpecialActor.Load('@',1)
ret 0

:Math_keepAngle
	while 0@ > 360.0
		0@ -= 360.0
	end
	while 0@ < 0.0
		0@ += 360.0
	end
ret 1 0@

:Math_keepRadian
	while 0@ > 6.2831853072
		0@ -= 6.2831853072
	end
	while 0@ < 0.0
		0@ += 6.2831853072
	end
ret 1 0@

:Math_angleToRadian
	0@ *= _pi
	0@ /= 180.0
ret 1 0@

:Math_radianToAngle
	0@ *= 180.0
	0@ /= _pi
ret 1 0@

:Math_Module
	int 28@ 
	int 30@ 

	float 29@ = Math.IntToFloat_LsL(30@)

	float 0@ = Math.IntToFloat_LsL(28@)
		  0@ /= 29@
	int   0@ = Math.FloatToInt_LsL(0@)

	int   1@ = 28@
	int	  2@ = 0@
		  2@ *= 30@
		  1@ -= 2@
	
return

:Math4_Module
	int 0@ 
	int 1@ 

	float 2@ = Math.IntToFloat_LsL(1@)

	float 3@ = Math.IntToFloat_LsL(0@)
		  3@ /= 2@
	int   3@ = Math.FloatToInt_LsL(3@)

	int   4@ = 0@
	int	  5@ = 3@
		  5@ *= 1@
		  4@ -= 5@
ret 2 3@ 4@

:InputNumberAndroid
	preRenderMenu()

	if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
	then
		if VK_Left()
		then NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID -= 1
		end
		if VK_Right()
		then NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID += 1
		end
		if ParaAdelante()
		then NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID -= 5
		end
		if ParaAtras()
		then NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID += 5
		end
	end

	if VK_Minus()
	then rs()
	end

	if NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID == 1
	then NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID = 4
	end
	if NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID == 5
	then NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID = 2
	end

	if NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID == 6
	then NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID = 9
	end
	if NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID == 10
	then NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID = 7
	end

	if NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID == 11
	then NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID = 14
	end
	if NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID == 15
	then NUM_PRESSED_AT_ANDROID = 12
	end

	if and

                                then 2@ = 0x46 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 5
                                then 2@ = 0x47 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 6
                                then 2@ = 0x48 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 7
                                then 2@ = 0x4A 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 8
                                then 2@ = 0x4B 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 9
                                then 2@ = 0x4C 
                                end

                                if 24@ == 0
                                then 23@ = -1
                                end
                                23@ += 1
                                1@ = 23@
                                String_setCharAt() 

                                while not 14@ == -1
                                    get_mutex_var 14@ = IMPORT_TOUCH_X2 
                                    Wait0()
                                end
                            end
                        end

                        10@ += 21
                        11@ += 21
                        12@ += 1
                    end
                end

                if 13@ == 4 
                then
                    int 10@ = 220 
                    int 11@ = 241 
                    int 12@ = 1 

                    while 12@ <= 8

                        
                        
                        if 14@ == -1
                        then
                            break
                        else
                            if and
                                14@ >= 10@
                                14@ <= 11@
                            then
                                if 12@ == 1
                                then 2@ = 0x5A 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 2
                                then 2@ = 0x58 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 3
                                then 2@ = 0x43 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 4
                                then 2@ = 0x56 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 5
                                then 2@ = 0x42 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 6
                                then 2@ = 0x4E 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 7
                                then 2@ = 0x4D 
                                end
                                if 12@ == 8
                                then 2@ = 0x5F 
                                end

                                if 24@ == 0
                                then 23@ = -1
                                end
                                23@ += 1
                                1@ = 23@
                                String_setCharAt() 

                                while not 14@ == -1
                                    get_mutex_var 14@ = IMPORT_TOUCH_X2 
                                    Wait0()
                                end
                            end
                        end

                        10@ += 21
                        11@ += 21
                        12@ += 1
                    end
                end
               
            end
        end
    

    
        if 23@ >= 0
        then
            if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
            then
                if Key.IsPressed(0x08)
                then
                    1@ = 23@
                    2@ = 0x00
                    String_setCharAt() 
                    while Key.IsPressed(0x08)
                        wait0()
                    end
                    23@ -= 1
                end
            else
                int 14@, 15@
                
                get_mutex_var 14@ = IMPORT_TOUCH_X2 
                
                get_mutex_var 15@ = IMPORT_TOUCH_Y2 

                if and
                    14@ > 400
                    14@ <= 440

                    15@ >= 320
                    15@ <= 357
                then
                    1@ = 23@
                    2@ = 0x00
                    String_setCharAt() 

                    while not 14@ == -1
                        Wait0()
                        get_mutex_var 14@ = IMPORT_TOUCH_X2 
                    end
                    23@ -= 1
                end
                
            end
        end
    

    
        if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
        then
            if Key.IsPressed(0x0D) 
            then valueString()
            end
        else
            int 14@, 15@
            
            get_mutex_var 14@ = IMPORT_TOUCH_X2 
            
            get_mutex_var 15@ = IMPORT_TOUCH_Y2 

            if and
                14@ > 380
                14@ <= 420

                15@ >= 394
                15@ <= 431
            then
                valueString()

                while not 14@ == -1
                    Wait0()
                    get_mutex_var 14@ = IMPORT_TOUCH_X2 
                end
                23@ -= 1
            end
        end
    

    
        if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
        then
            if Key.IsPressed(0x20)
            then 18@ = -1
            end
        else
            if Menu_Return()
            then 18@ = -1
            end
        end
    

    
    Text.SetWrapX(480.0)
    Text.SetCenter(true)
    if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    then
        Text.SetScale(1.0, 2.0)
        Text.Display(325.0, 350.0, 'M0000WY')
    else 
        Text.SetScale(2.0, 4.0)
        Text.Display(325.0, 300.0, 'M0000WY')
    end
return

:GiveWeaponAndAmmo 

	fixMagicPointer()
	Model.Load(1@)
	repeat
		Wait0()
	until Model.Available(1@)

	if 0@ == -1
	then
		Actor.setGiveWeaponAndAmmo(hPlayer, 2@, 3@)
	else

		Actor.setGiveWeaponAndAmmo(0@, 2@, 3@)
	end
	
	Model.Release(1@)
ret 0

:GiveWeaponAndAmmoB 

	fixMagicPointer()
	call @Weapon_GetModelID 1 1@ result 10@
	Model.Load(10@)
	Model.Requested()
	repeat
		Wait0()
	until Model.Available(10@)

	if 0@ == -1
	then
		Actor.setGiveWeaponAndAmmo(hPlayer, 1@, 2@)
	else
		if Actor.Defined(0@)
		then Actor.setGiveWeaponAndAmmo(0@, 1@, 2@)
		end
	end
	
	Model.Release(10@)
ret 0

        Frenar1()

:PrintFloatXY
	

	Math.FloatToInt_LsL(1@, 0@)
	0087: 2@ = 0@ 
	2@ *= 1000.0
	if 2@ < 0
	then 2@ *= -1.0
	end

	while 2@ > 100000.0
		2@ -= 100000.0
	end
	while 2@ > 10000.0
		2@ -= 10000.0
	end
	while 2@ > 5000.0
		2@ -= 5000.0
	end
	while 2@ > 2000.0
		2@ -= 2000.0
	end
	while 2@ > 1000.0
		2@ -= 1000.0
	end

	Math.FloatToInt_LsL(2@, 2@)
	Text.SetWrapX(630.0)
    Text.SetRightJustify(true) 
    
    Text.SetOutline(1, 0, 0, 0, 200)
    Text.SetFont(Font.Pricedown)
    Text.SetScale(0.45, 1.8)
return

:MemoryWrite
	int 0@ 
	int 1@ 
	int 2@ 

    0DD5: CURRENT_PLATFORM = get_platform
    if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    then Memory.Write(0@, 1@, 2@, false)
    else
    	if 1@ > 4
    	then
    		for 3@ = 0 to 1@ step 4
    			2402: write_memory_with_offset 0@ offset 3@ size 4 value 2@
    		end
    	else
    		0DD9: write_mem_addr 0@ value 2@ size 1@ add_ib 0 protect 0
    	end
    end	
ret 0

:MemoryRead

	int 2@ 

    0DD5: CURRENT_PLATFORM = get_platform
    if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS

    else 0DD8: 2@ = write_mem_addr 0@ size 1@ add_ib 0
    end
ret 1 2@

:ActorDefinidoInferior
	if SPS_NUM_ACTORS > 0
	then
		repeat
			SPS_INDEX_ACTORS--

			if SPS_INDEX_ACTORS < 1
			then SPS_INDEX_ACTORS = SPS_NUM_ACTORS
			end
			
			call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_HANDLE result SPS_ACTOR

		until Actor.Defined(SPS_ACTOR)
	else
		SPS_NUM_ACTORS = 0
		SPS_INDEX_ACTORS = 0
		SPS_ACTOR = 0
	end
return

:ActorDefinidoSuperior
	if SPS_NUM_ACTORS > 0
	then
		repeat
			SPS_INDEX_ACTORS++

			if SPS_INDEX_ACTORS > SPS_NUM_ACTORS
			then SPS_INDEX_ACTORS = 1
			end
			
			call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_HANDLE result SPS_ACTOR

		until Actor.Defined(SPS_ACTOR)
	else
		SPS_NUM_ACTORS = 0
		SPS_INDEX_ACTORS = 0
		SPS_ACTOR = 0
	end
return

:Search_Slot_Available_Actor
	fixMagicPointer()

	int 0@ = 1 

	while 0@ <= SPS_NUM_ACTORS
		SPS_INDEX_ACTORS = 0@

		call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 SPS_INDEX_ACTORS B_ACTOR_HANDLE result SPS_ACTOR
		if or
			0@ == 0
			not Actor.Defined(SPS_ACTOR)
		then
			0@ *= -1 
			break
		end
		
		0@ += 1  
	end

	if 0@ < 0 
	then
		0@ *= -1 
		SPS_INDEX_ACTORS = 0@
	else
		
		SPS_INDEX_ACTORS = SPS_NUM_ACTORS
		SPS_NUM_ACTORS++
		SPS_INDEX_ACTORS++
	end

ret 1 0@

:SPS_Get_Total_Actor
	fixMagicPointer()

	int 0@ = 0 
	int 10@ = 0

	while 0@ <= SPS_NUM_ACTORS
		call @SPS_Array_Actor_Get 2 0@ B_ACTOR_HANDLE result SPS_ACTOR
		
		if Actor.Defined(SPS_ACTOR)
		then 10@ += 1
		end

		0@ += 1
	end
ret 1 10@

:SMX_Get_Index_Actor
	
	fixMagicPointer()

	int 15@ = 0 
	int 20@ = false

	while 15@ <= SMX_NUM_ACTORS
		call @SMX_Array_Actor_Get 2 15@ B_ACTOR_ID result 20@

		if 20@ == 0@
		then
			ret 1 15@
			break
		end

		15@ += 1
	end
ret 1 false

		
		

		

		
		

:SPS_Array_Actor_Get
	
	

	10@ = 0@ * ACTOR_NUM_PROPERTIES
	10@ += 1@
	10@ *= 4

	fixMagicPointer()

    2401: read_memory_with_offset SPS_BUFFER_ACTORS offset 10@ size 4 store_to 20@
ret 1 20@

:SPS_Array_Actor_Set
	
	
	

	10@ = 0@ * ACTOR_NUM_PROPERTIES
	10@ += 1@
	10@ *= 4
	fixMagicPointer()

	2402: write_memory_with_offset SPS_BUFFER_ACTORS offset 10@ size 4 value 2@
ret 0

:SMX_Array_Actor_Get
	
	

	10@ = 0@ * ACTOR_NUM_PROPERTIES
	10@ += 1@
	10@ *= 4
	fixMagicPointer()

    2401: read_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_ACTORS offset 10@ size 4 store_to 20@
ret 1 20@

:SMX_Array_Actor_Set
	
	
	

	10@ = 0@ * ACTOR_NUM_PROPERTIES
	10@ += 1@
	10@ *= 4
	fixMagicPointer()

	2402: write_memory_with_offset SMX_BUFFER_ACTORS offset 10@ size 4 value 2@
ret 0

:iluminar_al_actor

	if Actor.Defined(SPS_ACTOR)
	then
		if FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE == FOCUS_LIGHT_NIGHT

			Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, SPS_ACTOR, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0)

			Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, SPS_ACTOR, -1.0, 0.0, 1.0)

			Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, SPS_ACTOR, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
			Fx.DrawShadow(SHADOW_TEXTURE_TYPE.EXPLOSION, __Af, __Bf, __Cf, 0.0, 1.0, 0xCC, 0xaa, 0x00, 0xff)
		end

		if FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE == FOCUS_LIGHT_DAY
		then
			Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, SPS_ACTOR, 0.0, 1.0, 1.0)
			Fx.DrawLightWithRange(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, 255, 255,255,10.0)
			Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, SPS_ACTOR, 0.0, -1.0, 1.0)
			Fx.DrawLightWithRange(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, 255, 255,255,10.0)
			Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, SPS_ACTOR, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
			Fx.DrawShadow(SHADOW_TEXTURE_TYPE.EXPLOSION, __Af, __Bf, __Cf, 0.0, 1.0, 0x77, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff)
		end

		if FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE == FOCUS_LIGHT_NONE
		then
			Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, SPS_ACTOR, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
			Fx.DrawShadow(SHADOW_TEXTURE_TYPE.EXPLOSION, __Af, __Bf, __Cf, 0.0, 0.2, 0xFF, 0xff, 0x0, 0x0)
		end

		28@ = 90  
		29@ = 122 
		if VK_PressedOnce()
		then
			if FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE >= 2
			then FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE = FOCUS_LIGHT_NONE
			else FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE++
			end
		end
	else
		printf "~p~:iluminar_al_actor~s~~n~actor not defined"
	end
ret 0

:HeightElement
	fixMagicPointer()

	if Blip.Defined(hEntityHighlighter)
	then
		if EXIST_ELEMENT_ILUMINATED == ELEMENT_ILUMINATED_NONE
		then return
		end
		if EXIST_ELEMENT_ILUMINATED == ELEMENT_ILUMINATED_ACTOR
		then iluminar_al_actor()
		end
		if EXIST_ELEMENT_ILUMINATED == ELEMENT_ILUMINATED_VEHICLE
		then 
		end
		if EXIST_ELEMENT_ILUMINATED == ELEMENT_ILUMINATED_PLAYER
		then iluminar_al_jugador()
		end
	end
ret 0

:iluminar_al_jugador
	fixMagicPointer()
	if FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE == FOCUS_LIGHT_NIGHT
	then
		Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, hPlayer, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0)
		Fx.DrawLightWithRange(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, 255, 0 ,0,10.0)
		Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, hPlayer, -1.0, 0.0, 1.0)
		Fx.DrawLightWithRange(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, 0,0, 255,10.0)
		Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, hPlayer, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
		Fx.DrawShadow(SHADOW_TEXTURE_TYPE.EXPLOSION, __Af, __Bf, __Cf, 0.0, 1.0, 0xCC, 0xaa, 0x00, 0xff)  
	end

	if FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE == FOCUS_LIGHT_DAY
	then
		Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, hPlayer, 0.0, 1.0, 1.0)
		Fx.DrawLightWithRange(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, 255, 255,255,10.0)
		Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, hPlayer, 0.0, -1.0, 1.0)
		Fx.DrawLightWithRange(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, 255, 255,255,10.0)
		Actor.GetPositionAndOffset(__Af, __Bf, __Cf, hPlayer, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0)
		Fx.DrawShadow(SHADOW_TEXTURE_TYPE.EXPLOSION, __Af, __Bf, __Cf, 0.0, 1.0, 0x77, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff)
	end

	28@ = 90  
	29@ = 122 
	if VK_PressedOnce()
	then
		if FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE >= 2
		then FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE = FOCUS_LIGHT_NONE
		else FOCUS_LIGHT_MODE++
		end
	end
ret 0

:recuperarSkinDelPlayer
	int 15@ = MODEL_PLAYER

	if 15@ >= 0
	then
		Model.Load(15@)
		repeat
			Wait0()
		until Model.Available(15@)
		Player.SetModel(hChar,15@)
	else
		if 15@ >= -500
		then
			15@ -= 500
			LoadSpecialActor()
		else
			15@ *= -1
			15@ -= 500
			call @CustomSkin4 1 15@
		end

		repeat
			Wait0()
		until SpecialActor.Available(1)
		Player.SetModel(hChar,#SPECIAL01)
	end
return

:Buffer_Var_Set
    int 0@,1@,2@

	0@ *= 4

	call @label_addr 1 @temp_var 2@

    2@ += 0@

    0DD5: 20@ = get_platform
	if 20@ == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
	then Memory.Write(2@, 4, 1@, false)
	else 0DD9: write_mem_addr 2@ value 1@ size 4 add_ib 0 protect 0
	end
ret 0

:Buffer_Var_Get
    int 0@,1@

	0@ *= 4

	call @label_addr 1 @temp_var 1@

    1@ += 0@
    
    0DD5: 20@ = get_platform
	if 20@ == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
    then 0@ = Memory.Read(1@, 4, false)
    else 0DD8: 0@ = read_mem_addr 1@ size 4 add_ib 0
    end
ret 1 0@

:bset_actor
    int 0@,1@,2@,3@

	0@ *= 4

	1@ *= 17

	1@ *= 4
	
	0@ += 1@ 

	3@ = SPS_BUFFER_ACTORS
    3@ += 0@

    call @MemoryWrite 3 3@ emINT32 2@
	
return

:bget_actor
    int 0@,1@,2@,3@

	
	0@ *= 4

	1@ *= 17
	1@ *= 4
	
	0@ += 1@ 

	3@ = SPS_BUFFER_ACTORS

    3@ += 0@

    call @MemoryRead 2 3@ emINT32 1@
    
    0@ = 1@
    
return

:label_addr
	

	0DD5: 20@ = get_platform
	if 20@ == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
	then 0AC6: 1@ = label_addr 0@
	else 0DD0: 1@ = label_addr 0@
	end
ret 1 1@

:getMagicPointer
	get_var_pointer 0@ = var &0

	call @label_addr 1 @bufferVarsPrivates 1@

	sub_int_lvar_from_int_lvar 1@ -= 0@
	1@ /= 4
	int_add 0@ = 1@ + 64
ret 1 0@

:fixMagicPointer
	call @getMagicPointer 0 30@
return

:VK_Ctrl_PressedOnce
	File_Chech_Exist()
	if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
	then
		if Key.IsPressed(VK.Ctrl)
		then
			if VK_CTRL_LOCK == 0
			then
				VK_CTRL_LOCK = 1
				return
			end
		else
			VK_CTRL_LOCK = 0
		end
	else
		if Widget.IsPressed(54) 
		then
			if VK_CTRL_LOCK == 0
			then
				VK_CTRL_LOCK = 1
				return
			end
		else
			VK_CTRL_LOCK = 0
		end
	end
return

:VK_PressedOnce
	PRESSE_DONCE_OFFSET = PRESSE_DONCE_WINDOWS * 4
	PRESSE_DONCE_OFFSET += VK_BUFFER
  call @MemoryRead 2 PRESSE_DONCE_OFFSET 4 VK_BUFFER_CURRENT_STATE

	if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
	then
		if Key.IsPressed(PRESSE_DONCE_WINDOWS)
		then
			if VK_BUFFER_CURRENT_STATE == 0
			then
				VK_BUFFER_CURRENT_STATE = 1
				call @MemoryWrite 3 PRESSE_DONCE_OFFSET 4 VK_BUFFER_CURRENT_STATE
				return_true
				return
			end
		else
			VK_BUFFER_CURRENT_STATE = 0
		end
	else
		if Widget.IsPressed(PRESSE_DONCE_ANDROID)
		then
			if VK_BUFFER_CURRENT_STATE == 0
			then
				VK_BUFFER_CURRENT_STATE = 1
				call @MemoryWrite 3 PRESSE_DONCE_OFFSET 4 VK_BUFFER_CURRENT_STATE
				return_true
				return
			end
		else
			VK_BUFFER_CURRENT_STATE = 0
		end
	end
	call @MemoryWrite 3 PRESSE_DONCE_OFFSET 4 VK_BUFFER_CURRENT_STATE
	return_false
return

	if NUMBER_PAGE > 1 
	then MovimientoVerticalDelMenu()
	end

	MovimientoHorizontalDelMenu() 
	

	_SELECTED = Menu.GetItemSelected(hPanel)

	:Menu_Select
	0DD5: CURRENT_PLATFORM = get_platform
	if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
	then
		if bit_is_true DYOS_FLAGS DEBUG_MODE
		then
			if Key.IsPressed(1)
			then
				if and
					DEBUG_CURSOR_X >= 36.0
					DEBUG_CURSOR_X <= 180.0
					DEBUG_CURSOR_Y >= 160.0
					DEBUG_CURSOR_Y <= 420.0
				then
					DYOS_HELP_ID = 0
					return
				end
			end
		end
		if Key.IsPressed(VK.R)
		then
			DYOS_HELP_ID = 0
			return
		end
		return_false
	else
		if Widget.IsPressed(100) 
		then
			Actor.GetPosition(hPlayer, 0@,1@,2@)
			Audio.ReportEventAtPosition(0@,1@,2@, 1054)
			DYOS_HELP_ID = 0
			return
		end
	end
return

:Menu_Return
	
	
	_SELECTED = Menu.GetItemSelected(hPanel)
	WaitMenu()
	if VK_Exit()
	then
		Text.ClearHelp()
		0DD5: CURRENT_PLATFORM = get_platform
		if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_ANDROID
		then
			Actor.GetPosition(hPlayer, tempvar_X_coord,tempvar_Y_coord,tempvar_Z_coord)
			Audio.ReportEventAtPosition(tempvar_X_coord,tempvar_Y_coord,tempvar_Z_coord, 1054)
			return
		end
		if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_WINDOWS
		then return
		end
	end
return

:MovimientoVerticalDelMenu
	if 803A: not CURRENT_PAGE == NUMBER_PAGE
	then
		if VK_Right()
		then CURRENT_PAGE++
			while VK_Right()
				WaitMenu()
			end
		end
	end
	if not CURRENT_PAGE == 1
	then
		if VK_Left()
		then CURRENT_PAGE--
			while VK_Left()
				WaitMenu()
			end
		end
	end
return

:MovimientoHorizontalDelMenu 
	if CURRENT_PLATFORM == __PLATFORM_ANDROID
	then
		0@ = Menu.GetItemSelected(hPanel)
		if  Widget.IsPressed(97) 
		then
			0@--
			Actor.GetPosition(hPlayer, x,y,z)
			Audio.ReportEventAtPosition(x,y,z, 1055)
			Menu.SetActiveItem(hPanel, 0@)
			while Widget.IsPressed(97) 
				WaitMenu()
			end
		end
		if Widget.IsPressed(98) 
		then
			0@++
			Actor.GetPosition(hPlayer, x,y,z)
			Audio.ReportEventAtPosition(x,y,z, 1055)
			Menu.SetActiveItem(hPanel, 0@)
			while Widget.IsPressed(98) 
				WaitMenu()
			end
		end
	end
return

:Menu_Close_Forced
    if VK_Escape()
    then
    	VK_Take_Escape()

    	Blip.Remove(hEntityHighlighter)
		call @Buffer_Var_Get 1 B_VAR_MENU_DISPLAY = 0@
			
    	if 0@ == MENU_DISPLAY_NONE
    	then Menu_Display_Show()
    	end

    	return_true
    	return
    end
return

:Menu_Take_Return
	while Menu_Return()
		WaitMenu()
	end
return

:Menu_Take_Selection
	while Menu_Enter()
		WaitMenu()
	end
return

:FrenarPaginacion
	while MovimientoVerticalDelMenu()
		WaitMenu()
	end
return

:Menu_Take_Left
	while VK_Left()
		WaitMenu()
	end
return

:Menu_Take_Right
	while VK_Right()
		WaitMenu()
	end
return

:FrenoMenuVertical
	while VK_Left()
		WaitMenu()
	end
	while VK_Right()
		WaitMenu()
	end
return

:FixUpdate
    fixMagicPointer()

call @get_bit_status 2 PLAYER_FLAGS PLAYER_PROP_IMMUNITION_BULLETS __A
call @get_bit_status 2 PLAYER_FLAGS PLAYER_PROP_IMMUNITION_FIRE __B
call @get_bit_status 2 PLAYER_FLAGS PLAYER_PROP_IMMUNITION_EXPLOSION __C
call @get_bit_status 2 PLAYER_FLAGS PLAYER_PROP_IMMUNITION_COLLISION __D
call @get_bit_status 2 PLAYER_FLAGS PLAYER_PROP_IMMUNITION_MELEE __E

Actor.SetImmunities(hPlayer,__A,__B,__C,__D,__E)

Player.SetIgnoredByCops(hChar) = false
Player.SetIgnoredByEveryone(hChar) = false

if bit_is_true PLAYER_FLAGS PLAYER_PROP_BLEEDING
then Actor.SetBleeding(hPlayer) = true
end

call @HeightElement 0

return

:Wait0
    FixUpdate()
    wait 0
return

:WaitMenu
:WaitLoadingAtMenu
	FixUpdate()
	wait 0
	Menu_Print_Pagination()
return

:WaitPlis
    FixUpdate()
    int 0@ 
    int 1@ 
    
    int 2@ 
    int 3@ 
    int 4@ = 0@
    
    2@ = Game.GetCurrentTimeMs()
   
    while true
        3@ = Game.GetCurrentTimeMs()
        3@ -= 2@
        if 3@ > 4@
        then break
        end
        if 1@ == 0
        then Wait0()
        else WaitMenu()
        end
    end 
ret 0
